@Country NVARCHAR(225)

SELECT TOP 1
@AccountID = ab.AccountID ,
@UserName = ac.Username ,
@Country = co.Alpha2Code
FROM RFOperations.RFO_Accounts.AccountBase (NOLOCK) ab
JOIN RFOperations.RFO_Accounts.AccountRF (NOLOCK) rf ON rf.AccountID = ab.AccountID
JOIN RFOperations.Security.AccountSecurity (NOLOCK) ac ON ac.AccountID = ab.AccountID
JOIN RFOperations.RFO_Reference.Countries (NOLOCK) co ON co.CountryID = ab.CountryID
WHERE ab.AccountTypeID = 1
AND ab.AccountStatusID = 1
AND co.Alpha2Code = 'US'
AND rf.Active = 1
AND EXISTS ( SELECT 1
FROM RFOperations.Hybris.Autoship (NOLOCK) a
WHERE a.AccountID = ab.AccountID
AND a.AutoshipTypeID = 3
AND a.Active = 1 )

FROM Commissions.calcs.vwQualificationSummary v
WHERE ab.AccountID = v.AccountID
AND v.PeriodID = @CurrentOpenPeriod
AND v.SV >= 100
AND v.PSQV >= 600 )
ORDER BY NEWID()

[INFO ] 2018-03-21 19:50:23.500 DBUtil - QUERY TRIGGERED IS DECLARE @CurrentOpenPeriod INT = ( SELECT TOP 1
PeriodID
FROM Commissions.reference.Periods
WHERE ClosedDate IS NULL
ORDER BY PeriodID ASC
) ,
@AccountID INT ,
@UserName NVARCHAR(225) ,
@Country NVARCHAR(225)

SELECT TOP 1
@AccountID = ab.AccountID ,
@UserName = ac.Username ,
@Country = co.Alpha2Code
FROM RFOperations.RFO_Accounts.AccountBase (NOLOCK) ab
JOIN RFOperations.RFO_Accounts.AccountRF (NOLOCK) rf ON rf.AccountID = ab.AccountID
JOIN RFOperations.Security.AccountSecurity (NOLOCK) ac ON ac.AccountID = ab.AccountID
JOIN RFOperations.RFO_Reference.Countries (NOLOCK) co ON co.CountryID = ab.CountryID
WHERE ab.AccountTypeID = 1
AND ab.AccountStatusID = 1
AND co.Alpha2Code = 'US'
AND rf.Active = 1
AND EXISTS ( SELECT 1
FROM RFOperations.Hybris.Autoship (NOLOCK) a
WHERE a.AccountID = ab.AccountID
AND a.AutoshipTypeID = 3
AND a.Active = 1 )
AND EXISTS ( SELECT 1
FROM Commissions.calcs.vwQualificationSummary v
WHERE ab.AccountID = v.AccountID
AND v.PeriodID = @CurrentOpenPeriod
AND v.SV >= 100
AND v.PSQV >= 600 )
ORDER BY NEWID()

SELECT ISNULL(@AccountID, 1496) AccountID ,
ISNULL(@UserName, 'skincareconsultants@gmail.com') UserName ,
ISNULL(@Country, 'US') Country ,
@CurrentOpenPeriod CurrentOpenPeriod

[INFO ] 2018-03-21 20:14:06.123 DBUtil - QUERY TRIGGERED IS DECLARE @CurrentOpenPeriod INT = ( SELECT TOP 1
PeriodID
FROM Commissions.reference.Periods
WHERE ClosedDate IS NULL
ORDER BY PeriodID ASC
) ,
@AccountID INT ,
@UserName NVARCHAR(225) ,
@Country NVARCHAR(225)

SELECT TOP 1
@AccountID = ab.AccountID ,
@UserName = ac.Username ,
@Country = co.Alpha2Code
FROM RFOperations.RFO_Accounts.AccountBase (NOLOCK) ab
JOIN RFOperations.RFO_Accounts.AccountRF (NOLOCK) rf ON rf.AccountID = ab.AccountID
JOIN RFOperations.Security.AccountSecurity (NOLOCK) ac ON ac.AccountID = ab.AccountID
JOIN RFOperations.RFO_Reference.Countries (NOLOCK) co ON co.CountryID = ab.CountryID
WHERE ab.AccountTypeID = 1
AND ab.AccountStatusID = 1
AND co.Alpha2Code = 'US'
AND rf.Active = 1
AND EXISTS ( SELECT 1
FROM RFOperations.Hybris.Autoship (NOLOCK) a
WHERE a.AccountID = ab.AccountID
AND a.AutoshipTypeID = 3
AND a.Active = 1 )
AND EXISTS ( SELECT 1
FROM Commissions.calcs.vwQualificationSummary v
WHERE ab.AccountID = v.AccountID
AND v.PeriodID = @CurrentOpenPeriod
AND v.SV >= 100
AND v.PSQV >= 600 )
ORDER BY NEWID()

SELECT ISNULL(@AccountID, 1496) AccountID ,
ISNULL(@UserName, 'skincareconsultants@gmail.com') UserName ,
ISNULL(@Country, 'US') Country ,
@CurrentOpenPeriod CurrentOpenPeriod

EOMONTH(DATEADD(MONTH,-1, GETDATE()))) AND CAST(GETDATE() AS DATE) AND ( ( ro.AccountID = @AccountID AND ab.AccountTypeID = 1) OR ( ro.ConsultantID = @AccountID AND ab.AccountTypeID = 3)) GROUP BY PeriodID
FROM Commissions.reference.Periods
WHERE ClosedDate IS NULL
ORDER BY PeriodID ASC
) ,
@AccountID INT ,
@UserName NVARCHAR(225) ,
@Country NVARCHAR(225)

SELECT TOP 1
@AccountID = ab.AccountID ,
@UserName = ac.Username ,
@Country = co.Alpha2Code
FROM RFOperations.RFO_Accounts.AccountBase (NOLOCK) ab
JOIN RFOperations.RFO_Accounts.AccountRF (NOLOCK) rf ON rf.AccountID = ab.AccountID
JOIN RFOperations.Security.AccountSecurity (NOLOCK) ac ON ac.AccountID = ab.AccountID
JOIN RFOperations.RFO_Reference.Countries (NOLOCK) co ON co.CountryID = ab.CountryID
WHERE ab.AccountTypeID = 1
AND ab.AccountStatusID = 1
AND co.Alpha2Code = 'US'
AND rf.Active = 1
AND EXISTS ( SELECT 1
FROM RFOperations.Hybris.Autoship (NOLOCK) a
WHERE a.AccountID = ab.AccountID
AND a.AutoshipTypeID = 3
AND a.Active = 1 )
AND EXISTS ( SELECT 1
FROM Commissions.calcs.vwQualificationSummary v
WHERE ab.AccountID = v.AccountID
AND v.PeriodID = @CurrentOpenPeriod
AND v.SV >= 100
AND v.PSQV >= 600 )
ORDER BY NEWID()
